<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прицеп.html>прице́п</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pricép</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прицеп.html>прице́па</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прицеп.html>прице́пы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прицеп.html>прице́пов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>trailer <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">vehicle towed behind another</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***прицепить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прицепить.html>прицепи́ть</a> (13637)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-цепи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-cepítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прицепить.html>прицепи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pricepítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">прицепля́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hitch <i>(to)</i>, to hook <i>(on to)</i>, <i>(railroad cars)</i> to couple <i>(to)</i>, <i>(locomotive)</i> to tie on <i>(to)</i>, to make fast <i>(to)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>(brooch, bow etc)</i> to pin <i>(on to)</i>, to fasten <i>(to)</i>, to tack <i>(to)</i>, to tag <i>(on to)</i></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>це<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:пить.html>пи́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:причал.html>прича́л</a> (6175)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:причал.html>прича́л</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pričál</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:причал.html>прича́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:причал.html>прича́лы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:причал.html>прича́лов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pier, mooring, berth, quay, dock, wharf, marina</li></ol>

Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>при-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-чал-</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ча́лить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čálitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>  to tie up (at), to moor (to)</li></ol>

***причастие.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>прича́стие</a> (27771)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:часть.html>часть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">častʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">part</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μετοχή</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">metokhḗ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">participium</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>прича́стие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pričástije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>прича́стия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>прича́стия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>прича́стий</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:причастный.html>прича́стный</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">grammar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> participle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">субстантиви́рованное <b><a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>прича́стие</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">substantivírovannoje <b>pričástije</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">substantivized participle (participle that functions as a noun)</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">religion</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> communion; Eucharist (ceremony, sacrament, or substances)</li></ol>

***причем.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:причем.html>причём</a> (906)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:причем.html>причём</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pričóm</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>moreover, and, at that, with
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:причем.html>причём</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:известный.html>изве́стно</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pričóm</b> izvéstno, što</i> ― <span class="e-translation">it being known that</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:причем.html>причём</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:каждый.html>ка́ждый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>них</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наполненный.html>напо́лнен</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:различный.html>разли́чным</a> конте́нтом</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pričóm</b> káždyj iz nix napólnen razlíčnym kontɛ́ntom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">with each of them being filled with a different content.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Usually not translated, but a following finite verb form is often translated as a present participle.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́том</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pri étom</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">da i</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вместе.html>вме́сте</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>тем</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vméste s tem</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>тому́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">k tomú že</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***прическа.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прическа.html>прическа</a> (6186)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbative of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:причесать.html>причеса́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pričesátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to comb, to brush</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru">причёска</strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pričóska</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прическа.html>причёски</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прическа.html>причёски</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прическа.html>причёсок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>haircut, coiffure, hairdo, hair dress, hair style</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:причинивший.html>причини́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pričinívšij</span>)

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:причинивший.html>причини́вший</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:действительный.html>Действи́тельное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>прича́стие</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:прошедший.html>проше́дшего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4a.

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:числить.html>чи́слить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">číslitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:причислить.html>причи́слить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pričíslitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:причислять.html>причисля́ть</a></b>)

<li>to attach <i>(to)</i></li></ol>
